# claude — a handwritten pipeline-stress / coverage suite.
#
# This suite is for *testing the pp2lp pipeline*, not for staying green.  It
# deliberately spans the whole rule space (every PP family) and the whole
# proof-size span (one-rule leaves → 200+-rule proofs), AND it probes the known
# frontier: set-equality / equality-congruence, arithmetic antisymmetry and
# double-negation (AR4/AR7/AR8), INS over rewritten hyps, NAT membership, and
# existential/quantifier shapes REPLAY mishandles.  Authored by hand, grouped by
# what each section tests.
#
# INVARIANT: every goal is a genuine theorem submitted to PP as the BARE goal —
# no hypotheses, no goal-as-hypothesis self-promotion.  PP proves it outright,
# closing the goal's free variables universally and inferring their types from
# context.  A goal PP cannot prove produces no .trace and is rejected at gen time
# (see the guardrail in gen_traces), so it does not belong here.  (Mind PP's
# parser: `<=>` binds tighter than `&`, and `=>` is left-associative —
# parenthesise accordingly, e.g. `(a & b) <=> (b & a)`, `x<=y => (y<=x => x=y)`.)
#
# Format: name | kind | goal
#   prop  — bare identifiers are propositional variables
#   expr  — bare identifiers are expression variables (sets / functions / ints)
#
# `goals.txt` is the source of truth — regenerate with `pp2lp gen claude`,
# check with `pp2lp run claude`.  Coverage notes (→ RULE) are intended targets;
# measure actual firings from the generated `.replay` files.  Some goals are
# theorems pp2lp cannot yet *translate* (Farkas, AR4/AR7/AR8, …); those fail at
# the lambdapi-check stage, not at PP — a signal about the pipeline frontier.

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# A. Propositional connectives — AND / OR / NOT, tiny → medium  (AND*, OR*, NOT*)
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# leaves (1–3 rules)

# identity / idempotence
p_imp_self        | prop | a => a
p_iff_self        | prop | a <=> a
p_and_idem        | prop | (a & a) <=> a
p_or_idem         | prop | a or a <=> a

# commutativity
p_and_comm        | prop | (a & b) <=> (b & a)
p_or_comm         | prop | a or b <=> b or a
p_iff_comm        | prop | (a <=> b) <=> (b <=> a)

# associativity
p_and_assoc       | prop | ((a & b) & c) <=> (a & (b & c))
p_or_assoc        | prop | (a or b) or c <=> a or (b or c)

# distributivity (both directions)
p_distrib_ao      | prop | (a & (b or c)) <=> ((a & b) or (a & c))
p_distrib_oa      | prop | (a or (b & c)) <=> ((a or b) & (a or c))

# absorption
p_absorb_and      | prop | (a & (a or b)) <=> a
p_absorb_or       | prop | a or (a & b) <=> a

# De Morgan (2- and 3-ary)
p_demorgan_and    | prop | not(a & b) <=> not(a) or not(b)
p_demorgan_or     | prop | (not (a or b)) <=> ((not a) & (not b))
p_demorgan_and3   | prop | not(a & b & c) <=> not(a) or not(b) or not(c)
p_demorgan_or3    | prop | (not ((a or b) or c)) <=> (((not a) & (not b)) & (not c))

# negation laws
p_dneg_elim       | prop | not(not(a)) => a
p_dneg_intro      | prop | a => not(not(a))
p_tneg            | prop | not(not(not(a))) => not(a)
p_excluded_middle | prop | a or not(a)
p_noncontra       | prop | not(a & not(a))

# bigger conjunction / disjunction shapes

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# B. Implication structure — IMP family, medium → large
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

imp_mp            | prop | a & (a => b) => b
imp_mt            | prop | (a => b) & not(b) => not(a)
imp_contrapos     | prop | (a => b) <=> (not(b) => not(a))
imp_curry         | prop | ((a & b) => c) <=> (a => (b => c))
imp_permute       | prop | (a => (b => c)) => (b => (a => c))
imp_to_or         | prop | (a => b) => not(a) or b
imp_from_or       | prop | not(a) or b => (a => b)
imp_neg           | prop | not(a => b) => a & not(b)
imp_peirce        | prop | ((a => b) => a) => a
imp_dist          | prop | (a => b => c) => ((a => b) => (a => c))
imp_cases         | prop | (a => c) & (b => c) => (a or b => c)
imp_syll          | prop | (a => b) & (b => c) => (a => c)
imp_syll4         | prop | (a => b) & (b => c) & (c => d) => (a => d)
imp_syll5         | prop | (a => b) & (b => c) & (c => d) & (d => e) => (a => e)
imp_chain_use     | prop | a & (a => b) & (b => c) & (c => d) => d

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# C. Equivalence — EQV family
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

eqv_sym           | prop | (a <=> b) => (b <=> a)
eqv_trans         | prop | (a <=> b) & (b <=> c) => (a <=> c)
eqv_trans4        | prop | (a <=> b) & (b <=> c) & (c <=> d) => (a <=> d)
eqv_to_imp        | prop | (a <=> b) => (a => b) & (b => a)
eqv_from_imp      | prop | (a => b) & (b => a) => (a <=> b)
eqv_neg_both      | prop | (a <=> b) <=> (not(a) <=> not(b))
eqv_neg_shift     | prop | (not(a) <=> b) <=> (a <=> not(b))
eqv_mp            | prop | a & (a <=> b) => b
eqv_cong_and      | prop | (a <=> b) => ((a & c) <=> (b & c))
# non-trivial equiv work (these don't collapse to a hypothesis match → EQV1/EQV2)
eqv_contra        | prop | not(p <=> p) => q
eqv_self_neg      | prop | not(p <=> not(p))
eqv_mutual        | prop | ((a => b) & (b => a)) <=> (a <=> b)
eqv_iff_split     | prop | (a <=> b) <=> ((a => b) & (b => a))

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# D. Equality — EVR / OPR / EQC / ECTR / EQS, tiny → large
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

eq_refl           | expr | x = x
eq_sym            | expr | x = y => y = x
eq_trans          | expr | x = y & y = z => x = z
eq_chain4         | expr | w = x & x = y & y = z => w = z
eq_chain5         | expr | v = w & w = x & x = y & y = z => v = z
eq_chain6         | expr | u = v & v = w & w = x & x = y & y = z => u = z
eq_fun_cong       | expr | x = y => f(x) = f(y)
eq_fun_cong2      | expr | x = y => f(g(x)) = f(g(y))
eq_fun_arg2       | expr | x = y => f(z, x) = f(z, y)
eq_fun_chain      | expr | f(x) = g(y) & g(y) = h(z) => f(x) = h(z)
eq_fun_deep       | expr | f(g(h(x))) = w & h(x) = y & g(y) = z => f(z) = w
eq_subst_mem      | expr | x = y & x: s => y: s
eq_subst_mem_sym  | expr | x = y & y: s => x: s
eq_subst_neg      | expr | x = y & not(x: s) => not(y: s)
eq_subst_arith    | expr | x = y & x <= z => y <= z
eq_subst_two      | expr | x = y & z = w & x: s & z: t => y: s & w: t
# set equality (→ EQS / eql_set)
eq_set_singleton  | expr | {x} = {x}
eq_set_pair       | expr | {x, y} = {x, y}
eq_set_union      | expr | s \/ t = s \/ t
eq_set_inter      | expr | s /\ t = s /\ t
eq_set_pair_swap  | expr | {x, y} = {y, x}
# equality contradiction (→ ECTR / FX / STOP)
eq_contra         | expr | x = y & not(x = y) => bfalse
eq_contra_chain   | expr | x = y & y = z & not(x = z) => bfalse

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# E. Membership & sets — AXM family, tiny → medium
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

set_in_singleton  | expr | x: {x}
set_in_pair_l     | expr | x: {x, y}
set_in_pair_r     | expr | y: {x, y}
set_in_triple     | expr | z: {x, y, z}
set_in_quad       | expr | w: {x, y, z, w}
set_in_union_l    | expr | x: s => x: s \/ t
set_in_union_r    | expr | x: t => x: s \/ t
set_in_inter      | expr | x: s & x: t => x: s /\ t
set_in_inter_l    | expr | x: s /\ t => x: s
set_in_inter_r    | expr | x: s /\ t => x: t
set_inter_to_union| expr | x: s /\ t => x: s \/ t
set_in_pow        | expr | s: POW(s)
set_empty_pow     | expr | {} : POW(s)

# subset (→ AXM / NRM, small → medium)
sub_refl          | expr | s <: s
sub_trans         | expr | s <: t & t <: u => s <: u
sub_trans4        | expr | s <: t & t <: u & u <: v => s <: v
sub_inter_l       | expr | s /\ t <: s
sub_inter_r       | expr | s /\ t <: t
sub_union_l       | expr | s <: s \/ t
sub_union_r       | expr | t <: s \/ t
sub_inter_glb     | expr | u <: s & u <: t => u <: s /\ t
sub_union_lub     | expr | s <: u & t <: u => s \/ t <: u
sub_empty         | expr | {} <: s
sub_singleton     | expr | x: s => {x} <: s
sub_singleton_iff | expr | x: s <=> {x} <: s
sub_pair          | expr | {x} <: s & {y} <: s => {x, y} <: s
sub_in_pow        | expr | s: POW(t) <=> s <: t
sub_union_mono    | expr | s <: t => s \/ u <: t \/ u
sub_inter_mono    | expr | s <: t => s /\ u <: t /\ u
sub_self_union    | expr | s \/ s <: s
sub_self_inter    | expr | s <: s /\ s

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# G. Universal quantifier — ALL / NRM family, medium → large
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

all_refl_body     | expr | !x.(x: s => x: s)
all_inter_intro   | expr | !x.(x: s => x: a) & !x.(x: s => x: b) => !x.(x: s => x: a & x: b)
all_distrib_and   | expr | !x.((x: s => (x: a & x: b))) <=> (!x.((x: s => x: a)) & !x.((x: s => x: b)))
all_nested        | expr | !x.(!y.((x: s => (y: t => x: s))))
all_swap          | expr | !x.!y.(x: s & y: t => x, y: r) => !y.!x.(y: t & x: s => x, y: r)
all_point_mono    | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) & a: s => a: t
all_point_trans   | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) & !x.(x: t => x: u) => !x.(x: s => x: u)

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# H. Existential quantifier — XST family (deliberately broad; coverage gap)
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

xst_eq            | expr | #x.(x = a)
xst_mem           | expr | a: s => #x.(x: s)
xst_witness       | expr | a: s & a: t => #x.(x: s & x: t)
xst_weaken        | expr | a: s => #x.(x: s or x: t)
xst_eq_mem        | expr | a: s => #x.(x = a & x: s)
xst_from_all      | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) & a: s => #x.(x: t)
xst_pair          | expr | a: s & b: t => #x.#y.(x: s & y: t)
xst_swap          | expr | #x.#y.(x: s & y: t) => #y.#x.(x: s & y: t)
xst_in_dom        | expr | a: dom(f) => #x.(x: dom(f))
xst_app           | expr | a: dom(f) & f(a) = b => #x.(f(x) = b)
xst_refute        | expr | a: s & not(a: t) => #x.(x: s & not(x: t))
# existential under a universal (witness is the ∀-bound var): HO-unification
# frontier — AXM9_1 inh_tuple witness + ALL7/XST8 chain Res won't resolve (open).
xst_under_all     | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) => !x.(x: s => #y.(y: t))

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# I. Boolean — BOOL family (concrete btrue/bfalse only; PP can't do a: BOOL)
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

bool_eq_self      | expr | x = TRUE => x = TRUE
bool_subst        | expr | x = TRUE & x = y => y = TRUE

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# J. Arithmetic — AR family, tiny → medium
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

ar_leq_refl       | expr | x <= x
ar_leq_trans      | expr | x <= y & y <= z => x <= z
ar_leq_trans4     | expr | x <= y & y <= z & z <= w => x <= w
ar_leq_antisym    | expr | x <= y & y <= x => x = y
ar_lt_trans       | expr | x < y & y < z => x < z
ar_lt_to_leq      | expr | x < y => x <= y
ar_leq_to_lt      | expr | x <= y & not(x = y) => x < y
ar_add_comm       | expr | x + y = y + x
ar_add_assoc      | expr | (x + y) + z = x + (y + z)
ar_add_zero_l     | expr | 0 + x = x
ar_add_zero_r     | expr | x + 0 = x
ar_sub_zero       | expr | x - 0 = x
ar_sub_self       | expr | x - x = 0
ar_sub_add        | expr | (x - y) + y = x
ar_add_sub        | expr | (x + y) - y = x
ar_add_mono_r     | expr | x <= y => x + z <= y + z
ar_add_mono_l     | expr | x <= y => z + x <= z + y
ar_add_mono2      | expr | x <= y & z <= w => x + z <= y + w
ar_add_comm_leq   | expr | x + y <= z => y + x <= z
ar_add_assoc_leq  | expr | (x + y) + z <= w => x + (y + z) <= w
ar_bounds_neg     | expr | x <= 0 & y <= 0 => x + y <= 0
ar_bounds_pos     | expr | 0 <= x & 0 <= y => 0 <= x + y
ar_bounds_pos3    | expr | 0 <= x & 0 <= y & 0 <= z => 0 <= x + y + z
ar_sub_leq        | expr | x - y <= 0 => x <= y
ar_leq_sub        | expr | x + y <= z => x <= z - y
ar_add_pos        | expr | 0 <= y => x <= x + y
ar_sub_pos        | expr | 0 <= y => x - y <= x

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# K. Quantified arithmetic & contradiction — NRM-arith / INS / FX / STOP
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

qar_leq_refl      | expr | !x.(x <= x)
qar_antisym       | expr | !x.(!y.((x <= y => (y <= x => x = y))))
qar_trans         | expr | !x.(!y.(!z.((x <= y => (y <= z => x <= z)))))
qar_ins           | expr | !x.(x + 1 <= y => not(y <= x))
ctr_prop          | prop | a & not(a) => bfalse
ctr_mem           | expr | x: s & not(x: s) => bfalse
ctr_subst         | expr | x = y & x: s & not(y: s) => bfalse
ctr_all           | expr | !x.(x: s => not(x: t)) & a: s & a: t => bfalse
ctr_all_pos       | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) & a: s & not(a: t) => bfalse
ctr_arith         | expr | x <= y & y <= x & not(x = y) => bfalse

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# L. FRONTIER: set equality & equality congruence  (EQS / ECTR / eql_set)
#    These force structural set-equality reasoning, the documented LP gap —
#    expected ✗.  Kept to exercise the EQS/ECTR emit + check path.
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

eqc_subst_set     | expr | s = t & x: s => x: t
eqc_union_cong    | expr | s = t => s \/ u = t \/ u
eqc_inter_cong    | expr | s = t => s /\ u = t /\ u
eqc_pair_swap     | expr | {x, y} = {y, x}
eqc_subset_antisym| expr | s <: t & t <: s => s = t
eqc_pow_mono      | expr | s <: t => POW(s) <: POW(t)
eqc_app_cong_set  | expr | s = t => f(s) = f(t)

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# M. FRONTIER: arithmetic — antisymmetry, double-negation, cancellation, NAT
#    Hits AR4/AR7/AR8 (need the solver's witness, never in the replay) and the
#    NAT-membership blow-up (RLIMIT_AS / timeout capped).  Expected ✗/⚠.
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

arf_antisym_neg   | expr | !x.!y.(-x + y <= 0 & x - y <= 0 => x = y)
arf_antisym_neg2  | expr | !x.!y.(x - y <= 0 & -x + y <= 0 => y = x)
arf_neg_neg       | expr | !x.(not(not(x <= y)) => x <= y)
arf_cancel_r      | expr | x + z = y + z => x = y

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# N. FRONTIER: INS contradiction over arithmetic-rewritten hypotheses
#    PP rewrites hyps before the INS leaf; find_ins_contradiction may miss the
#    structural match or pick the wrong compound witness (→ NRM24/27-30).
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

nar_ins1          | expr | !x.(x + 1 <= y => not(y <= x))
nar_ins_succ      | expr | !x.(not(x + 1 <= x))
nar_nat_quant     | expr | !x.(x: NAT => 0 <= x)
# x + x normalises to the coefficient form 2*x — the `*` parser gap (now fixed,
# desugared to x+x); this goal now reaches the next gap, PP's `[ARITH] <FAUX>`
# solver terminal (not in rule_db).
nar_leq_zero      | expr | !x.(x <= 0 => x + x <= 0)

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# O. FRONTIER: existential / compound-binder shapes REPLAY mishandles (XST2/6)
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

xstf_triple       | expr | a: s & b: t & c: u => #x.#y.#z.(x: s & y: t & z: u)
xstf_pair_binder  | expr | a, b: r => #(x, y).(x, y: r)
# type-checks through the new NRM3_1/NRM23_1 lemmas; remaining blocker is the
# existential-under-universal HO-unification frontier (shared with xst_under_all):
# AXM9_1 hardcodes the inh_tuple witness AND the ALL7/XST8 chain Res won't resolve.
xstf_all_exists   | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) => !x.(x: s => #y.(x = y & y: t))
xstf_dom_witness  | expr | a: dom(f) & f(a) = b => #x.(x: dom(f) & f(x) = b)
xstf_swap_compound| expr | #(x, y).(x, y: r) => #(y, x).(y, x: r)

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# P. Deep / large proofs — push the high end of the size span (NRM/Res chains)
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

big_eq_chain8     | expr | a1 = a2 & a2 = a3 & a3 = a4 & a4 = a5 & a5 = a6 & a6 = a7 & a7 = a8 => a1 = a8
big_sub_chain6    | expr | s <: t & t <: u & u <: v & v <: w & w <: r => s <: r
big_leq_chain6    | expr | x <= y & y <= z & z <= w & w <= v & v <= r => x <= r
# cascade ≥3 conjuncts: was right-assoc A∧(B∧C) vs NRM7's left-assoc peel — fixed
# by making IMP1_1 list-preserving (mk_res, not mk_1) so the ⋀-list stays flat.
big_mixed         | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) & !x.(x: t => x: u) & !x.(x: u => x: v) => !x.(x: s => x: v)

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 2026-06-09 expansion: sections Q–Z take the suite to ~500 goals.
# Same charter — pipeline stress + bug hunting, not a guaranteed-green gate.
# Sections X (ARITH solver terminal) and Y (AXM*-discharged chain elements)
# are the test beds for the ARITH certificate and the trust-free AXM*_1 work.
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# Q. Propositional, deeper and wider — classical shapes, ⇔ algebra
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

q2_imp_join       | prop | (a => c) & (b => c) & (a or b) => c
q2_case_split     | prop | (a => b) & (not(a) => b) => b
q2_peirce         | prop | ((a => b) => a) => a
q2_contrapos      | prop | (a => b) => (not(b) => not(a))
q2_contrapos_rev  | prop | (not(b) => not(a)) => (a => b)
q2_modus_tollens  | prop | (a => b) & not(b) => not(a)
q2_imp_trans3     | prop | (a => b) & (b => c) & (c => d) => (a => d)
q2_or4_comm       | prop | a or b or c or d => d or c or b or a
q2_and4_comm      | prop | a & b & c & d => d & c & b & a
q2_or_idem3       | prop | a or a or a => a
q2_and_over_or    | prop | a & (b or c) => (a & b) or (a & c)
q2_or_over_and    | prop | (a or b) & (a or c) => a or (b & c)
q2_demorgan4      | prop | not(a or b or c or d) => not(a) & not(b) & not(c) & not(d)
q2_demorgan_mix   | prop | not(a & b) or not(c & d) => not(a & b & c & d)
q2_neg3           | prop | not(not(not(a))) => not(a)
q2_neg4           | prop | not(not(not(not(a)))) => a
q2_imp_weaken     | prop | a => (b => a)
q2_imp_swap_args  | prop | (a => (b => c)) => (b => (a => c))
q2_imp_dup        | prop | (a => (a => b)) => (a => b)
q2_curry          | prop | (a & b => c) => (a => (b => c))
q2_uncurry        | prop | (a => (b => c)) => (a & b => c)
q2_absorb_chain   | prop | a & (a or b) & (a or c) => a
q2_or_absorb_deep | prop | a or (a & b & c) => a
q2_xorish         | prop | (a or b) & not(a & b) & a => not(b)
q2_iff_or_cong    | prop | (a <=> b) => (a or c <=> b or c)
q2_iff_not_flip   | prop | (a <=> b) <=> (not(b) <=> not(a))
q2_iff_chain5     | prop | (a <=> b) & (b <=> c) & (c <=> d) & (d <=> e) => (a <=> e)
q2_iff_and_proj   | prop | ((a & b) <=> a) <=> (a => b)
q2_cond_join      | prop | (a => b) or (b => a)
q2_dn_imp         | prop | not(not(a => b)) => (not(not(a)) => not(not(b)))
q2_neg_imp_and    | prop | not(a => b) => a & not(b)
q2_and_neg_imp    | prop | a & not(b) => not(a => b)
q2_or_as_imp      | prop | (not(a) or b) <=> (a => b)
q2_parallel_cases | prop | (a => b) & (c => d) & (a or c) => b or d
q2_em             | prop | a or not(a)
q2_noncontra      | prop | not(a & not(a))
q2_imp_refl_deep  | prop | ((a => a) => b) => b
q2_weak_const     | prop | a & b => (c => a)
q2_or_intro_deep  | prop | a => ((a or b) or c) or d
q2_triple_mix     | prop | (a & b) or (a & c) or (a & d) => a
q2_wide_or8       | prop | a => a or b or c or d or e or g or h or i
q2_wide_and8      | prop | a & b & c & d & e & g & h & i => e
q2_release        | prop | (a => b & c) & a => c

# R. Universals, deeper — wide binder blocks, instantiation, monotone bodies

u2_all4_chain     | expr | !x.(x: a => x: b) & !x.(x: b => x: c) & !x.(x: c => x: d) & !x.(x: d => x: e) => !x.(x: a => x: e)
u2_all_and_or     | expr | !x.(x: s => x: a & x: b) => !x.(x: s => x: a or x: c)
u2_all_pair_proj  | expr | !x.!y.(x,y: r => x: s & y: t) => !x.!y.(x,y: r => y: t)

u2_all5_wide      | expr | !x.!y.!z.!v.!w.(x: a & y: b & z: c & v: d & w: e => x: a & w: e)
u2_all_const_body | expr | p => !x.!y.(x: s => p)
u2_all_inst2      | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) & a: s & b: s => a: t & b: t
u2_all_pair_inst  | expr | !x.!y.(x,y: r => y,x: q) & a,b: r => b,a: q

u2_mono_inter     | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) => !x.(x: s /\ u => x: t /\ u)
u2_all_neg_body   | expr | !x.(x: s => not(x: t)) & a: s & a: t => bfalse
u2_sub_then_all   | expr | s <: t & !x.(x: t => x: u) => !x.(x: s => x: u)
u2_deep_imp_inst  | expr | !x.(x: a => x: b => x: c => x: d) & a1: a & a1: b & a1: c => a1: d

u2_or_cases_all   | expr | !x.(x: s => x: a or x: b) & !x.(x: a => x: c) & !x.(x: b => x: c) => !x.(x: s => x: c)
u2_vacuous2       | expr | !x.!y.(x: s & not(x: s) => y: t)
u2_all_and_keep   | expr | p & !x.(x: s => x: t) => !x.(x: s => x: t) & p
u2_all_dom_inst   | expr | !x.(x: dom(f) => x: s) & a: dom(f) => a: s
u2_all_app_mem    | expr | !x.(x: dom(f) => f(x): t) & a: dom(f) => f(a): t
u2_all_app_eq     | expr | !x.(x: s => f(x) = g(x)) & a: s => f(a) = g(a)
u2_all_arith_body | expr | !x.(x: s => 0 <= x) & a: s => 0 <= a
u2_all_leq_bound  | expr | !x.(x: s => x <= y) & a: s => a <= y
u2_pair_sym_inst  | expr | !x.!y.(x,y: r => y,x: r) & a,b: r => b,a: r
u2_two_alls_inst  | expr | !x.(x: a => x: b) & !y.(y: b => y: c) & a1: a => a1: c
u2_rel_chain      | expr | !x.!y.(x,y: r => x,y: q) & !x.!y.(x,y: q => x,y: w) => !x.!y.(x,y: r => x,y: w)
u2_all_eq_body    | expr | !x.(x: s => x = a) & b: s => b = a
u2_all_fun_ext    | expr | !x.(f(x) = g(x)) => f(c) = g(c)
u2_all_pow_mem    | expr | s <: t => !x.(x: POW(s) => x: POW(t))
u2_all_notnot     | expr | !x.(x: s => not(not(x: t))) => !x.(x: s => x: t)
u2_split_nested   | expr | !x.(x: s => (x: a & x: b) & x: c) => !x.(x: s => x: b)
u2_or_antecedent  | expr | !x.(x: s or x: t => x: u) => !x.(x: s => x: u)

st_inter_sub_l    | expr | s /\ t <: s

st_eq_mem_both    | expr | s = t & x: s & y: t => x: t & y: s

st_card_self      | expr | card(s) = card(s)

st_inter_self_sub | expr | s <: s /\ s

fn_app_self       | expr | x: dom(f) => f(x) = f(x)
fn_app_cong       | expr | x = y & x: dom(f) => f(x) = f(y)

q3_chain5         | prop | (a => b) & (b => c) & (c => d) & (d => e) => (a => e)

q3_and_rotate     | prop | a & b & c => c & a & b
q3_or_rotate      | prop | a or b or c => c or a or b
q3_dn_and         | prop | not(not(a)) & not(not(b)) => a & b
u3_inst_three     | expr | !x.(x: s => x: t) & a: s & b: s & c: s => a: t & b: t & c: t
u3_two_layer      | expr | !x.(x: a => x: b) & !x.(x: b => x: c) & d1: a & d2: a => d1: c & d2: c
u3_body_and4      | expr | !x.(x: s => x: a & x: b & x: c & x: d) & e1: s => e1: c
u3_neg_inst       | expr | !x.(not(x: s) or x: t) & a: s => a: t
x3_wit_and_eq     | expr | a: s & a = b => #x.(x: s & x = b)
x3_wit_app        | expr | f(a) = c => #x.#y.(f(x) = y)
x3_wit_chain      | expr | a: s & !x.(x: s => x: t) => #x.(x: s) & #x.(x: t)
ec2_chain6        | expr | c1 = c2 & c2 = c3 & c3 = c4 & c4 = c5 & c5 = c6 => c1 = c6
ec2_star_join     | expr | a = z & b = z & c = z => a = b & b = c
ec2_app_both      | expr | x = y & f(x) = g(y) & f(x) = w => g(y) = w
ec2_mem_two       | expr | x = y & x: s & x: t => y: s & y: t
a3_leq_plus2      | expr | x <= y & 0 <= z => x <= y + z
a3_minus_mono     | expr | x <= y => x - z <= y - z
a3_chain_mixed    | expr | x <= y & y < z & z <= w => x < w
a3_zero_middle    | expr | x <= 0 & 0 <= z => x - 1 <= z
a3_lit_spread     | expr | x <= 1 & 1 <= y => x <= y
a3_plus_swap_leq  | expr | x + y + z <= w => z + y + x <= w
st2_mem_inter3    | expr | x: s /\ t /\ u => x: t
st2_mem_union3    | expr | x: s => x: u \/ t \/ s
st2_eq_singleton  | expr | a = b => {a} = {b}
st2_pair_both     | expr | x: {a, b} & not(x = a) => x = b
fn2_app_four      | expr | f(a) = b & f(c) = d & a: dom(f) & c: dom(f) => f(a) = b & f(c) = d

# W. Solver terminals & positional substitution (added 2026-06-10)
#    Probes for newly-wired machinery: the ARITH Farkas closer (→ ARITH),
#    the EGALITE equality-prover terminal (→ EGALITE), slot-positional
#    NRM20/21 pins and NRM26 drops, and literal folding in the generated
#    sum-equality proofs (AR3/AR3_F with folded constants).
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# ARITH Farkas certificates: multiplier 3, two-variable, constants > 1.
narf_triple       | expr | !x.(x <= 0 => x + x + x <= 0)
narf_neg_triple   | expr | !x.(0 <= x => 0 <= x + x + x)
narf_two_var      | expr | !x.!y.(x <= 0 & y <= 0 => x + y + x <= 0)
narf_const_gap    | expr | !x.(x <= 3 => x + x <= 9)
narf_const_slack  | expr | !x.(x <= 2 => x + x + x <= 8)
narf_opp_pair     | expr | !x.!y.(x + y <= 0 & 0 <= y => x <= 1)

# EGALITE: equality-prover terminal (universal hyps used modulo equalities).
# The bare !x-hyp forms (e.g. `!x.(x: s => x: u) & s = t & a: t => a: u`)
# prove fine in PP but REPLAY fails to convert their traces — use the
# subset-expansion shapes (the st_eq_pow trigger context) instead.
egal_sub_self     | expr | s = t => s <: t

# NRM20/21 positional pins: witness = another bound var, RHS orientation,
# real (non-⊤) conjunct prefixes, mid-list equality.
x2_eq_wits_rev    | expr | #x.#y.(y = x)
x2_app_graph_rev  | expr | a: s & b = f(a) => #x.#y.(x: s & y = f(x))
x2_two_app        | expr | f(a) = b => #x.#y.(y = f(x))
x3_mid_wit        | expr | a: s & f(a) = c => #x.#y.(x: s & f(x) = y & y = c)
x3_three_wits     | expr | f(a) = b => #x.#y.#z.(f(x) = y & y = z)

# NRM26 positional drops: re-quantified universals with reordered binders
# leave the unused binder at slot 0 / 1 / last.
u2_all_swap2      | expr | !x.!y.(x: a => y: b) => !y.!x.(x: a => y: b)
u2_all_rotate     | expr | !x.!y.!z.(x: a => y: b => z: c) => !y.!z.!x.(x: a => y: b => z: c)
u2_all_mid_drop   | expr | !x.!y.!z.(x: a => z: c) => !z.!x.(x: a => z: c)

# X. COVERAGE PUSH (added 2026-06-10, second wave): targets the 47 rules no
#    replay fires (BOOL*, EAXM*, EQC*, EIMP5*, EVR1/2/11, ECTR5/6, FX1/2,
#    VR2, NRM2/4/16-18/27/28/30, ALL2, XST2/51/61, AR2/5/6/13) and the 15
#    thin ones.  Sections X.* by family; expected mostly ✓ — a ✗ here is a
#    pipeline finding, see the session notes.
#
#    Post-run findings (all surviving goals ✓):
#    - The bl_/eqx_ probes prove in ONE AXM8 step: the promoted self-proof
#      hypothesis matches the goal before any bool()/equality-special rule
#      can fire.  BOOL11-52, EAXM*, EQC1/2, EIMP5*, ECTR5/6, EVR11 stay
#      REPLAY-unreachable under this harness (they need hyp/goal
#      normalisation to diverge); bl_* still validates that `bool(P)`
#      round-trips the whole pipeline.  Newly fired instead: AR2, EVR1,
#      EVR2, FX1, NRM2, NRM4, XST51.
#    - fk_sandwich and qs_pin_{zero,first,second,both} hit a SECOND
#      upstream REPLAY failure mode: the tool writes
#      `**** impossible case in rplMainX ****` mid-file.  Classified
#      E_REPLAY_TRUNCATED and gen-dropped, like the continuation drops.
#    - 14 further REPLAY-truncation drops (literal-constant pins
#      `#x.(x = 5)`, arith-pinned existentials, vacuous-binder nestings —
#      see the gen output).

# X.a — bool(P) operator (→ BOOL11-52; PP's bool-valued predicates)
bl_via_eq         | expr | x = y => bool(x = z) = bool(y = z)

# X.b — equality-prover special rules: commuted-orientation hyps (EQC1/2,
# EAXM1/2), reflexivity specials (EVR1/2/11), commuted-imp (EIMP51/52),

# Z. BARE-KIND PROBES (added 2026-06-10, third wave).  `bprop`/`bexpr` drop
#    the goal-as-hypothesis self-promotion, so PP must genuinely PROVE the
#    formula — the special rule families the harness could never reach
#    (BOOL11-52, EAXM*, EQC, EIMP5*, EVR11, ECTR5/6, AR5/6/7/13, VR2, FX2,
#    EQV2, XST2/61, NRM16-18) get their first real shot at firing.  PP may
#    fail outright on some (no hypothesis to lean on) — gen drops those.
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# Z post-run findings (third wave; suite 1114✓/0✗ after fixes):
# - EGALITE now fires from GENERATED replays (za_zero_sum, ze_comm_neg,
#   ze_ectr_arith, ze_imp_comm{,2}) — the emit path previously validated
#   only against a hand-completed replay is now corpus-covered.  za_zero_sum
#   additionally needed a literal-fold bridge in the equality-store evidence
#   (rewritten antecedent `1<=0` vs in-scope `1-(x+x)<=0` under x:=0).
# - EAXM31/EAXM32 are goal-closing LEAVES (hyp = the goal's equality
#   commuted); rule_db had them as 1-child passthroughs (ze_comm_neg ended
#   its replay at [EAXM32]).  EAXM1, AR5, EQV2 also fire for the first time.
# - All 13 zb_ bool() goals FAIL AT PP itself when bare — PP cannot prove
#   bool(P)-round-trips without a hypothesis to match, so BOOL11-52 remain
#   unreachable end-to-end (now established as a PP limitation, not a
#   harness artifact).  zq_swap2 likewise unprovable bare.
# - Rule coverage after the wave: 103/138 rule_db names fire; the remaining
#   unfired set is BOOL*, half the EAXM/EQC/EIMP5/ECTR5-6 family, NRM16-18,
#   NRM27/28/30, ALL2, AR6/7/13, VR2, FX2, XST2/61.

gemini_demorgan_and      | prop | not(a & b) <=> (not(a) or not(b))
gemini_demorgan_or       | prop | not(a or b) <=> (not(a) & not(b))

gemini_distrib_and_or    | prop | (a or (b & c)) <=> ((a or b) & (a or c))

gemini_nested_app_eq     | expr | f(x) = g(y) & g(y) = h(z) => f(x) = h(z)

# >>> GX GENERATED BLOCK (regenerable; see /tmp/gen_goals.py) >>>
# GX. Parameterized size-sweep families — scaling / performance benchmark.
#     Dense linear chains + width sweeps + super-linear case-splits across the
#     families PP proves bare and REPLAY does not truncate, swept over size so
#     proof length scales with the parameter.  Generated, not hand-authored;
#     every goal is a genuine theorem.  Arithmetic sweeps are capped at PP's
#     provable band.
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
gx_syll3                   | prop | (a1 => a2) & (a2 => a3) => (a1 => a3)
gx_syll4                   | prop | (a1 => a2) & (a2 => a3) & (a3 => a4) => (a1 => a4)

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# GXC. Coverage probes — shapes aimed at rules the suite never fired, adapted
#      from og/prv/apero triggers (negated quantifiers → ALL1/2, XST1/2;
#      VRAI/FAUX → FX1/2; BOOL split; reversed/commuted equality → OPR/EQC/ECTR;
#      vacuous binders → NRM).  Probes: non-theorems here get pruned at gen.
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# negated-universal goal (→ ALL2): inner body is a contradiction, so the
# universal is false and its negation is the theorem.
gxc_nall_self        | expr | not(!x.(not(x = x)))
gxc_nall_self2       | expr | not(!x.!y.(not(x = x)))
gxc_nall_mem         | expr | not(!x.(x: s & not(x: s)))
gxc_nall_pred        | expr | not(!x.(p(x) & not(p(x))))
gxc_nall_le          | expr | not(!x.(x <= x => not(x <= x)))
# negated-universal hypothesis (→ ALL1): tautological consequent keeps it provable
gxc_nall_h1          | prop | not(!x.!y.(x = y)) => p or not(p)
gxc_nall_h2          | expr | not(!x.(x = x)) => (q => q)
gxc_nall_h3          | expr | not(!x.(x: s)) => p or not(p)
gxc_nall_h4          | expr | not(!x.!y.(x: s)) => (a = a)
# negated-existential goal (→ XST2): no witness can satisfy a contradiction
gxc_nxst_self        | expr | not(#x.(not(x = x)))
gxc_nxst_mem         | expr | not(#x.(x: s & not(x: s)))
gxc_nxst_pred        | expr | not(#x.(p(x) & not(p(x))))
gxc_nxst_two         | expr | not(#x.#y.(p(x,y) & not(p(x,y))))
gxc_nxst_le          | expr | not(#x.(x < x))
# negated-existential hypothesis (→ XST1)
gxc_nxst_h1          | expr | not(#x.(x = x)) => p or not(p)
gxc_nxst_h2          | expr | not(#x.(x: s)) => (q => q)
gxc_nxst_h3          | expr | not(#x.#y.(p(x,y))) => (a = a)
# VRAI / FAUX literals (→ FX1/FX2/VR2/VR3)
gxc_fx_nfaux         | prop | not(FAUX)
gxc_fx_nfaux_vrai    | prop | not(FAUX) => VRAI
gxc_fx_vrai          | prop | VRAI
gxc_fx_faux_any      | prop | FAUX => p
gxc_fx_faux_mem      | expr | FAUX => x: s
gxc_fx_vrai_and      | prop | VRAI & p => p
gxc_fx_or_vrai       | prop | p or VRAI
gxc_fx_nfaux_or      | prop | not(FAUX) or p
# boolean case analysis (→ BOOL*): x ranges over BOOL
gxc_bool_split       | expr | x: BOOL => x = TRUE or x = FALSE
gxc_bool_not_true    | expr | x: BOOL & not(x = TRUE) => x = FALSE
gxc_bool_not_false   | expr | x: BOOL & not(x = FALSE) => x = TRUE
gxc_bool_true_mem    | expr | TRUE: BOOL
gxc_bool_false_mem   | expr | FALSE: BOOL
gxc_bool_from_eq     | expr | x = TRUE => x: BOOL
gxc_bool_neq         | expr | x: BOOL & y: BOOL & not(x = y) & not(x = TRUE) => y = TRUE
# reversed / commuted equality (→ OPR1/OPR2, EQC1/EQC2, EVR11)
gxc_eq_rev           | expr | a = b => b = a
gxc_eq_rev_app       | expr | f(x) = y => y = f(x)
gxc_eq_rev_chain     | expr | a = b & b = c => c = a
gxc_eq_rev_two       | expr | a = b & c = d => b = a & d = c
gxc_eq_rev_mem       | expr | a = b & a: s => b: s
gxc_eq_commute_h     | expr | b = a & a: s => b: s
# equality contradiction (→ ECTR1/ECTR5)
gxc_ectr_rev         | expr | a = b & not(b = a) => bfalse
gxc_ectr_chain       | expr | a = b & b = c & not(c = a) => bfalse
gxc_ectr_app         | expr | f(x) = y & not(y = f(x)) => bfalse
gxc_ectr_sym2        | expr | a = b & c = a & not(c = b) => bfalse
# vacuous / constant binders (→ NRM16-18, NRM4/8/9/11)
gxc_nrm_vac_all      | expr | !x.(a = a)
gxc_nrm_vac_all2     | expr | !x.!y.(a = a)
gxc_nrm_vac_mem      | expr | !x.(a: s) => a: s
gxc_nrm_vac_const    | expr | a: s => !x.(a: s)
gxc_nrm_const_imp    | expr | p => !x.(p)
# arithmetic identities (→ AR3/AR9/AR10/AR13)
gxc_ar_self_le       | expr | !x.(x <= x)
gxc_ar_eq_self       | expr | !x.(x = x)
gxc_ar_zero_le       | expr | !x.(0 <= x => 0 <= x)
gxc_ar_succ_lt       | expr | !x.(x < x + 1)
# truth rules (→ VR2/VR3)
gxc_vr2_nfvrai       | prop | FAUX => not(VRAI)
gxc_vr3_passthru     | prop | VRAI => (p or not(p))
gxc_vr3_self         | prop | VRAI => VRAI
# boolean equality antecedent — every orientation (→ BOOL11..52)
gxc_bool31           | expr | x: BOOL & not(x = TRUE) => x = FALSE
gxc_bool32           | expr | x: BOOL & not(x = FALSE) => x = TRUE
gxc_bool41           | expr | x: BOOL & not(TRUE = x) => x = FALSE
gxc_bool42           | expr | x: BOOL & not(FALSE = x) => x = TRUE
gxc_bool51           | prop | TRUE = FALSE => p
gxc_bool52           | prop | FALSE = TRUE => p
# equality-prover special shapes (→ EVR2/EVR11/EAXM2/EIMP51/EIMP52)
gxc_evr2_exfalso     | expr | FAUX => not(x = x)
gxc_evr11_lit        | expr | 1 = 2 => p
gxc_evr11_lit2       | expr | 3 = 5 => x: s
gxc_eaxm2            | expr | a = b => (not(b = a) => p)
gxc_eimp51           | expr | not(b = a) => (not(a = b) => (p or not(p)))
gxc_eimp52           | expr | b = a => (a = b => (p or not(p)))
# pair-equality decomposition (→ EQC1/EQC2)
gxc_eqc2             | expr | (a, b) = (c, d) => a = c
gxc_eqc2b            | expr | (a, b) = (c, d) => b = d
gxc_eqc1             | expr | not((a, b) = (c, d)) => (not(a = c) or not(b = d))
# equality-rewrite contradiction (→ ECTR1/ECTR5)
gxc_ectr1            | expr | b: s & not(a: s) => (a = b => bfalse)

# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# GXF. Frontier probes — bare theorems over under-exercised B constructs
#      (relation inverse/composition/dom/ran/image/override/restriction,
#      function arrows, cardinality/finiteness, intervals, multiplication/
#      power/div/mod, min/max/SIGMA, comprehension/lambda, POW1, generalized
#      union/inter).  Intent: surface emit/translate/check failures.
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# ── relations: inverse (~) ──
gxf_inv_mem          | expr | (a, b): r => (b, a): r~
gxf_inv_back         | expr | (b, a): r~ => (a, b): r
gxf_inv_invol        | expr | (a, b): r => (a, b): r~~
gxf_inv_dom_ran      | expr | a: dom(r) => a: ran(r~)
gxf_inv_ran_dom      | expr | b: ran(r) => b: dom(r~)
gxf_inv_eq_ran       | expr | dom(r~) = ran(r)
gxf_inv_comp         | expr | (a, b): r & (b, c): s => (c, a): (r ; s)~
# ── relations: composition (;) ──
gxf_comp_mem         | expr | (a, b): r & (b, c): s => (a, c): (r ; s)
gxf_comp_unfold      | expr | (a, c): (r ; s) => #x.((a, x): r & (x, c): s)
gxf_comp_dom         | expr | (a, c): (r ; s) => a: dom(r)
gxf_comp_assoc_mem   | expr | (a, b): r & (b, c): s & (c, d): q => (a, d): (r ; (s ; q))
# ── relations: dom / ran ──
gxf_dom_mem          | expr | (a, b): r => a: dom(r)
gxf_ran_mem          | expr | (a, b): r => b: ran(r)
gxf_dom_exists       | expr | a: dom(r) => #y.((a, y): r)
gxf_ran_exists       | expr | b: ran(r) => #x.((x, b): r)
gxf_dom_sub          | expr | dom(r) <: s & (a, b): r => a: s
gxf_dom_mono         | expr | r <: s => dom(r) <: dom(s)
gxf_ran_mono         | expr | r <: s => ran(r) <: ran(s)
# ── relations: image r[s] ──
gxf_img_mem          | expr | a: s & (a, b): r => b: r[s]
gxf_img_unfold       | expr | b: r[s] => #x.(x: s & (x, b): r)
gxf_img_mono         | expr | s <: t => r[s] <: r[t]
# ── relations: override (<+) ──
gxf_over_right       | expr | (a, b): s => (a, b): (r <+ s)
gxf_over_dom         | expr | a: dom(r) => a: dom(r <+ s)
# ── relations: restrictions (<| |>) ──
gxf_domr_intro       | expr | a: s & (a, b): r => (a, b): (s <| r)
gxf_domr_elim        | expr | (a, b): (s <| r) => a: s
gxf_domr_elim2       | expr | (a, b): (s <| r) => (a, b): r
gxf_ranr_intro       | expr | (a, b): r & b: s => (a, b): (r |> s)
gxf_ranr_elim        | expr | (a, b): (r |> s) => b: s
# ── functions: arrows & application ──
gxf_pfun_app         | expr | f: s +-> t & a: dom(f) => f(a): t
gxf_tfun_app         | expr | f: s --> t & a: s => f(a): t
gxf_tfun_dom         | expr | f: s --> t => dom(f) = s
gxf_tfun_comp        | expr | f: s --> t & g: t --> u & a: s => g(f(a)): u
gxf_inj_cancel       | expr | f: s >-> t & a: s & b: s & f(a) = f(b) => a = b
gxf_surj_ran         | expr | f: s -->> t => ran(f) = t
gxf_fun_mem_pair     | expr | f: s --> t & a: s => (a, f(a)): f
# ── cardinality & finiteness ──
gxf_fin_empty        | expr | {} : FIN(s)
gxf_fin_single       | expr | x: s => {x}: FIN(s)
# ── intervals (..) ──
gxf_intv_lo          | expr | a: c .. d => c <= a
gxf_intv_hi          | expr | a: c .. d => a <= d
gxf_intv_intro       | expr | c <= a & a <= d => a: c .. d
gxf_intv_iff         | expr | a: c .. d <=> (c <= a & a <= d)
gxf_intv_end_lo      | expr | c <= d => c: c .. d
gxf_intv_end_hi      | expr | c <= d => d: c .. d
gxf_intv_conc        | expr | x: 2 .. 5 => x <= 5
gxf_intv_sub         | expr | a <= b & c <= d & b <= c => a .. b <: a .. d
# ── arithmetic: multiplication ──
gxf_mul_zero_r       | expr | x * 0 = 0
gxf_mul_zero_l       | expr | 0 * x = 0
gxf_mul_one_r        | expr | x * 1 = x
gxf_mul_one_l        | expr | 1 * x = x
gxf_mul_assoc        | expr | (x * y) * z = x * (y * z)
gxf_mul_distrib      | expr | x * (y + z) = x * y + x * z
gxf_mul_two          | expr | 2 * x = x + x
gxf_mul_mono         | expr | 0 <= z & x <= y => x * z <= y * z
# ── arithmetic: power / div / mod ──
gxf_pow_zero         | expr | x ** 0 = 1
gxf_pow_one          | expr | x ** 1 = x
gxf_div_one          | expr | x / 1 = x
gxf_div_self         | expr | 0 < x => x / x = 1
gxf_mod_one          | expr | x mod 1 = 0
gxf_mod_self         | expr | 0 < x => x mod x = 0
# ── arithmetic: concrete computation (literal stress) ──
gxf_lit_add          | expr | 2 + 3 = 5
gxf_lit_mul          | expr | 7 * 6 = 42
gxf_lit_sub          | expr | 100 - 1 = 99
gxf_lit_big          | expr | 1000 + 2000 = 3000
gxf_lit_leq          | expr | 5 <= 12
gxf_lit_chain        | expr | x + 5 <= x + 7
# ── arithmetic: min / max / SIGMA ──
gxf_max_mem          | expr | s: FIN1(t) & x: s => x <= max(s)
gxf_min_mem          | expr | s: FIN1(t) & x: s => min(s) <= x
gxf_max_single       | expr | max({x}) = x
gxf_min_single       | expr | min({x}) = x
# ── set comprehension / lambda ──
gxf_lam_app          | expr | x: s => (%y.(y: s | y))(x) = x
# ── power set variants ──
gxf_pow1_sub         | expr | s: POW1(t) => s <: t
gxf_pow1_ne          | expr | s: POW1(t) => not(s = {})
gxf_pow_empty        | expr | {} : POW(s)
gxf_pow_self         | expr | s: POW(s)
gxf_pow_mono         | expr | s <: t => POW(s) <: POW(t)
# ── generalized union / inter ──
gxf_gunion_mem       | expr | s: S & x: s => x: union(S)
gxf_ginter_mem       | expr | s: S & x: inter(S) => x: s

# GXP/GXQ/GXE/GXN. Final amplifier — maps the pj1 pair-projection emit bug

gxc_comp3                  | expr | (x0, x1): r1 & (x1, x2): r2 & (x2, x3): r3 => (x0, x3): ((r1 ; r2) ; r3)
gxc_comp4                  | expr | (x0, x1): r1 & (x1, x2): r2 & (x2, x3): r3 & (x3, x4): r4 => (x0, x4): (((r1 ; r2) ; r3) ; r4)
gxc_comp5                  | expr | (x0, x1): r1 & (x1, x2): r2 & (x2, x3): r3 & (x3, x4): r4 & (x4, x5): r5 => (x0, x5): ((((r1 ; r2) ; r3) ; r4) ; r5)
gxc_comp6                  | expr | (x0, x1): r1 & (x1, x2): r2 & (x2, x3): r3 & (x3, x4): r4 & (x4, x5): r5 & (x5, x6): r6 => (x0, x6): (((((r1 ; r2) ; r3) ; r4) ; r5) ; r6)
gxc_comp7                  | expr | (x0, x1): r1 & (x1, x2): r2 & (x2, x3): r3 & (x3, x4): r4 & (x4, x5): r5 & (x5, x6): r6 & (x6, x7): r7 => (x0, x7): ((((((r1 ; r2) ; r3) ; r4) ; r5) ; r6) ; r7)
gxe_div_g                  | expr | 0 < y => x / y <= x / y
gxe_div_h                  | expr | z = x / y & z = w => w = x / y
gxe_div_le                 | expr | 0 < y & x <= w => x / y <= x / y
gxe_card_h                 | expr | n = card(s) & n = m => m = card(s)
gxn_fun_app2               | expr | f: s --> t & g: t --> u & a: s => g(f(a)): u
gxn_fun_pair               | expr | f: s --> t & a: s => (a, f(a)): f
gxn_rel_dom                | expr | r: s <-> t & (a, b): r => a: s
gxn_rel_ran                | expr | r: s <-> t & (a, b): r => b: t
gxn_pfun_uniq              | expr | f: s +-> t & (a, b): f & (a, c): f => b = c

# bm_* — binder-merge probes (Phase 2 of the curried-merge-rule work).  These
# exercise the §A.7–8 quantifier regroupement at sites flatten_binds reaches
# AND ones it cannot:
#   - relation identities (composition / inverse / dom / ran) whose proofs fan
#     out through branching quantifiers; the merges land in the main tree (ALL3
#     in a Res-chain continuation, exercised by branch_cont) or are flattened.
#   - universal-antecedent goals `(!x.#y.#z.…) ⇒ …`: PP runs the antecedent
#     through ALL7 and merges the per-tuple `#y.#z` inside a Res chain (`XST4_1`).
#     Under flatten_binds the chain merge is a no-op, so the emitter skips it
#     (Translate.chain_term); before that fix these were E_DISPATCH.
# bm_allxst reaches the E_INS frontier *after* the merge (a separate gap), so it
# stays red — kept as a frontier probe.
bm_rc_invcomp        | expr | (r ; s)~ = (s~ ; r~)
bm_comp_unfold2      | expr | (a, d): ((r ; s) ; t) => #x.#y.((a, x): r & (x, y): s & (y, d): t)
bm_comp_back2        | expr | (#x.#y.((a, x): r & (x, y): s & (y, d): t)) => (a, d): ((r ; s) ; t)
bm_comp_back         | expr | (#x.((a, x): r & (x, c): s)) => (a, c): (r ; s)
bm_dom_comp          | expr | dom(r ; s) <: dom(r)
bm_ran_comp          | expr | ran(r ; s) <: ran(s)
bm_allid             | expr | (!x.#y.#z.r(x,y,z)) => (!x.#y.#z.r(x,y,z))
bm_allweak           | expr | (!x.#y.#z.r(x,y,z)) => (!x.#y.#z.(r(x,y,z) or s))
bm_allconj           | expr | (!x.#y.#z.(r(x,y,z) & t(x))) => (!x.#y.#z.r(x,y,z))
bm_allxst            | expr | (!x.#y.#z.(p(x,y) & q(y,z))) => (!x.#y.p(x,y))
